Hydrogen Bonding: Many host molecules (e.g., cyclodextrins, calixarenes, crown ethers) can form hydrogen bonds with guest species, enabling selective recognition and displacement of the indicator.\n\n2. Electrostatic Interactions: Charged hosts (such as functionalized cyclodextrins or cucurbiturils) can interact with oppositely charged guests or indicators, providing strong and reversible binding.\n\n3. π-π Stacking: Aromatic hosts (e.g., calixarenes, pillararenes) can engage in π-π stacking with aromatic guest molecules or indicators, which is particularly useful for sensing aromatic analytes.\n\n4.
